  <script type="text/javascript">
   var id_language_by_location = 0;
var id_currency_by_location = 0;
var p_status = $.cookie('iplang_ps');

function iplang_popup(force_show)
{
  $.get('/modules/iplang/ajax.php', { action: 'detect',force_show:force_show},
  	function(result){
      if (result.show_popup == '0')
      {
        id_language_by_location = result.id_language_by_location;
        id_currency_by_location = result.id_currency_by_location;

        $.fancybox.open([
							{
								href: '#iplang-popup',
                'closeBtn':false
							}
						], {
							padding: 0
						});

            $("#iplang-lng").val(id_language_by_location);  
            $("#iplang-currency").val(id_currency_by_location);
            
            if (force_show)
              $("#iplang-country").val(result.default_country).change();
            else
              $("#iplang-country").val(result.id_country_code).change();
      }
      else if (result.force_redirect == '1')
      {
        id_language_by_location = result.id_language_by_location;
        id_currency_by_location = result.id_currency_by_location;
        
        $.ajax({
    		type: "POST",
    		headers: { "cache-control": "no-cache" },
    		url: baseDir + "index.php" + "?rand=" + new Date().getTime(),
    		data: "controller=change-currency&amp;id_currency="+ parseInt(id_currency_by_location),
    		success: function(msg)
    		{
          $.cookie("iplang_ps","shown", { expires: 365, path: '/' });
          $.cookie("iplang_country",result.id_country_code, { expires: 365, path: '/' });

          location.href = result.redirect_to;  
    		}
    	});
      }
  	},
    'json'
    );
 }

$(document).ready(function() {

if (p_status != 'shown')
{
  iplang_popup(0);
  $.cookie("iplang_ps","shown", { expires: 365, path: '/' });  
}

});
  </script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
         $(document).ready(function() {
    $("#iplang-popup-launcher").click(function(){
      $.fancybox.open([
				{
					href: '#iplang-popup',
          'closeBtn':false
				}
			], {
				padding: 0
			});
      $("#country-loader").html('&lt;img src="/modules/iplang/img/loader.gif"&gt;');
      
      $.get('/modules/iplang/ajax.php', { action: 'detect',force_show:1},
      function(result){
        id_language_by_location = result.id_language_by_location;
        id_currency_by_location = result.id_currency_by_location;
        
        $("#iplang-lng").val(id_language_by_location);  
        $("#iplang-currency").val(id_currency_by_location);
        
        $('#iplang-country option[value='+result.default_country+']').attr("selected","selected");
        
        t = $("#iplang-country").find('option:selected').text();
        
        $('#iplang-country').selectbox('change', result.default_country, t);
        
        $("#country-loader").html('');
      
        },
      'json'
      );
      return false;
    });
    
    $.get('/modules/iplang/ajax.php', { action: 'get-location',curr_lang:'en'},
      function(result){
         $("#iplang-popup-launcher").html(result.html);     
        },
      'json'
      );
    
    
  });
        </script>

     <script type="text/javascript">
      // 
  $(document).ready(function() {
  
  jQuery.fn.swap = function(b){ 
    b = jQuery(b)[0]; 
    var a = this[0]; 
    var t = a.parentNode.insertBefore(document.createTextNode(''), a); 
    b.parentNode.insertBefore(a, b); 
    t.parentNode.insertBefore(b, t); 
    t.parentNode.removeChild(t); 
    return this; 
};

  jQuery("#right_toolbar .shoppingcart").mouseenter(function () {
        //$("#right-minicart-wrapper").prepend($("#top-minicart-wrapper").html());
        $("#top-minicart-wrapper").swap("#right-minicart-wrapper");
        $("#right-minicart-wrapper").show();
        jQuery(this).find(".shopping_cart_mini").stop(true, true).fadeIn(200, "linear");
    });

    jQuery("#right_toolbar .shoppingcart").mouseleave(function () {
        jQuery(this).find(".shopping_cart_mini").stop(true, true).fadeOut(200, "linear");
        $("#right-minicart-wrapper").hide();
        $("#right-minicart-wrapper").swap("#top-minicart-wrapper");
    });
    
    
    $("#search-input").autocomplete({
        source:'/modules/tonycartslider/ajax_search.php',
        id:'ui-search-wrapper',
        minLength: 3,
        appendTo:'#autocomplete-results-wrapper',
        open: function(){
        $(this).autocomplete('widget').css('z-index', 5000);
        return false;
        },
        select: function(event, ui) {
          if (ui.item.link != '')
            document.location.href=ui.item.link;
        }
    });



  });
//
     </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function() {
  
 
  $("#iplang-popup .close-btn").click(function(){
    $.fancybox.close();
    return false;
  });
    var lng_rewrite = {"1":"http:\/\/www.flatsevenshop.com\/shirts\/","2":"http:\/\/www.flatsevenshop.com\/de\/shirts\/","3":"http:\/\/www.flatsevenshop.com\/gb\/shirts\/","4":"http:\/\/www.flatsevenshop.com\/ja\/shirts\/","6":"http:\/\/www.flatsevenshop.com\/zh\/shirts\/","7":"http:\/\/www.flatsevenshop.com\/fr\/shirts\/","8":"http:\/\/www.flatsevenshop.com\/br\/shirts\/","9":"http:\/\/www.flatsevenshop.com\/ru\/shirts\/","11":"http:\/\/www.flatsevenshop.com\/es\/shirts\/","13":"http:\/\/www.flatsevenshop.com\/it\/shirts\/"};
    
    $("#iplang-country").change(function(){
      var id = $(this).val();
      if (id == 0)
        return false;
      $("#lang-wrapper").html('&lt;img src="/modules/iplang/img/loader.gif"&gt;');
      $.get('/modules/iplang/ajax.php', { action: 'get-lng-selector',cid:id},
      	function(result){
          $("#lang-wrapper").html(result.content);
          $(".custom").selectbox();
      	},
        'json'
        );
    });
    
    $("#iplang-go").click(function(){
      var lng = $("#iplang-lng").val();
      var curr = $("#iplang-currency").val();
      var country = $("#iplang-country").val();
      
      $.ajax({
    		type: "POST",
    		headers: { "cache-control": "no-cache" },
    		url: baseDir + "index.php" + "?rand=" + new Date().getTime(),
    		data: "controller=change-currency&amp;id_currency="+ parseInt(curr),
    		success: function(msg)
    		{
          $.cookie("iplang_ps","shown", { expires: 365, path: '/' });
          $.cookie("iplang_country",country, { expires: 365, path: '/' });

          if (lng_rewrite[lng])
    			  location.href = lng_rewrite[lng];
          else
            location.href = baseDir;  
    		}
    	});
      
      return false;
    });
  });
   </script>

         <script type="text/javascript">
          $(document).ready(function() {
    $(".choose-vmode").click(function(){
      var vmode = $(this).attr('vmode');
      
      if (vmode == 'list')
      {
        $("#product_list").removeClass('vmode1').removeClass('vmode2').addClass('vmode2');
        $(".list-chooser").css('opacity','1');
        $(".grid-chooser").css('opacity','0.5');
      }
      else
      {
        $("#product_list").removeClass('vmode1').removeClass('vmode2').addClass('vmode1');
        $(".grid-chooser").css('opacity','1');
        $(".list-chooser").css('opacity','0.5');
      }  
      
      $.cookie("vmode",vmode, { expires: 365, path: '/' });    
      
      return false; 
    });
  });
         </script>

         <script type="text/javascript">
          jQuery(document).ready(function () {
    $(".compare-selector").click(function(){
     var checkbox = $(this).siblings("input[type=checkbox].comparator");
     checkbox.attr("checked", !checkbox.attr("checked"));
     checkbox.trigger('click');
     checkbox.attr("checked", !checkbox.attr("checked"));
      return false;
    });
  });
         </script>

         <script type="text/javascript">
          $(document).ready(function() {
    $(".choose-vmode").click(function(){
      var vmode = $(this).attr('vmode');
      
      if (vmode == 'list')
      {
        $("#product_list").removeClass('vmode1').removeClass('vmode2').addClass('vmode2');
        $(".list-chooser").css('opacity','1');
        $(".grid-chooser").css('opacity','0.5');
      }
      else
      {
        $("#product_list").removeClass('vmode1').removeClass('vmode2').addClass('vmode1');
        $(".grid-chooser").css('opacity','1');
        $(".list-chooser").css('opacity','0.5');
      }  
      
      $.cookie("vmode",vmode, { expires: 365, path: '/' });    
      
      return false; 
    });
  });
         </script>
         <div class="pull-right alignright ">
